At the one-hour mark, it's transformed into a beautiful warm vanilla, not too caramel-heavy at all.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="2035237" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=2035237#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent2035030" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":5,"winter":0,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":0,"sillage":0,"gender":null,"relation":null}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="5" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;" v-sticky=""><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260031">Cristinaaa</b><span class="vote-button-legend" content="2024-01-09" itemprop="datePublished" style="padding: 0 1rem;">01/09/24 12:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div itemprop="reviewBody" v-pre=""><p>First impression: I'm 30 min into wearing this fragrance for the first time. The most prominent notes upon first spray were almond, vanilla, and alcohol. The alcohol quickly dissipated and I'm left with an almondy-vanilla with hints of lactonic notes peeking through. When I press my nose against my skin, I can pick up on something that smells like play dough. However, the play dough smell becomes less obvious over time. Overall, I like this vanilla as it seems to be getting sweeter and denser the longer I wear it. There is also something airy about it. I'm going to hold on to my bottle for a few months and continue to test. I hate to say it, but I was initially reminded of Outremer vanilla ... however, Bianco Latte is certainly a stronger, more creamy vanilla. I'm hoping that once the fragrance macerates, it will be even richer and denser. Will update if my opinion changes.<br/>
<br/>
Update: I am smelling coconut in the opening. It makes the vanilla smell very synthetic - not at all like dense white chocolate/condensed milk. While I disagree that it smells like Pink Sugar, I do think this fragrance is reminiscent of perfumes from my younger days. <br/>
<br/>
After much consideration, I decided to sell my bottle. The fragrance did get richer and creamier the longer I had it. However, something about it just didn't feel like me. Maybe it was the intensely sweet vanilla - it was just too linear for my liking. I found myself craving something beyond just vanilla. Granted, I could have layered this fragrance with another - but I am of the belief that fragrances should be enjoyable on their own.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br/>
Oh my goodness gracious, this may be it! This has been on me for two hours now, and it reminds me of Demeter EggNog - but stronger, less powdery, and more... magical? Like its classy older cousin, who is ever so sweet and never snooty.<br/>
<br/>
On my skin I smell sweetened milk, vanilla, LIGHT musk, nutmeg, and... I'm guessing this is the coumarin, but there is a distinct fresh cherry tobacco fragrance. It's sweet, rich, and just a bit complex without overwhelming the senses. Being used to less expensive fragrances and body sprays this is SOOO strong! It's not overpowering, just more powerful than I'm used to... which is PERFECT, as I will need to save up for a full bottle, which will last longer since I'll need to use less! <br/>
<br/>
Longevity... still quite noticeable as a (strong) skin scent, 14 hours later! I got a bit on my sweater, and it's QUITE strong there as well! <br/>
<br/>
I said I'd know when I found what I've been looking for... I'm pretty sure this is it!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="2025410" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=2025410#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent2025288" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":0,"winter":0,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":3,"sillage":2,"gender":"female","relation":"have"}'></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;" v-sticky=""><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1318153">Foxzilla</b><span class="vote-button-legend" content="2024-01-08" itemprop="datePublished" style="padding: 0 1rem;">01/08/24 12:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div itemprop="reviewBody" v-pre=""><p>Woah, I finally get the hype! I'd been testing this for a while, but I never really enjoyed it. In fact, I didn't like it at all in the beginning. I thought it smelled like an atom bomb of play-doh, and that was it. But after going thru a sample vial, I finally tried it on thru the atomizer, and it changed the scent for me. I get a beautiful, enveloping caramel &amp; condensed milk / vanilla pudding vibe now, and the play-doh scent is now a balanced toasted almond note (that I enjoy). Like taking a bite of biscotti with sip of warm vanilla latte. But √ó1000. This scent is not for the faint of heart. It is incredibly strong and sweet, but in the best way. <br/>
<br/>
I'm not sure if it's the method of application, or just the distance at which I'm smelling it, but it really changed to a whole nother scent. When I smell my wrist close up, I still get that original stingy play-doh vibe, but from arm's/shirt's length, it's beautiful. And this one is a knock out! I like my fragrances strong, but I was still surprised by this one. I only need 2 half sprays to last me the whole day, and the spots on my skin still smell and _project_ after handwashings. Incredible. If only all scents could have this performance. If you're have issues with this one, try it on clothes, and try it from farther away. It'd be a shame for anyone to miss the true scent of this due to a difference of application. Word of warning tho -- this scent is VERY sweet. Those who don't enjoy sweet, gourmand, and/or vanilla scents, I would not recommend getting this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="2024541" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=2024541#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent2024348" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":1,"winter":0,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":0,"sillage":0,"gender":null,"relation":null}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="1" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Also very one dimensional, what you initially sniff is what you'll get for the next 6+ hours</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="2020325" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=2020325#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent2020121" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":1,"winter":1,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":2,"sillage":2,"gender":null,"relation":"have"}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="1" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div class="cell small-2" id="cc2018205" sticky-container=""><div v-sticky=""><div class="comments-avatar" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" style="position: relative;"><meta content="forumgames" itemprop="name"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1897248"><img alt="forumgames" class="comments-avatar" itemprop="image" loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1897248.jpg" style="opacity: 0.85;"/></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div class="ckNxM ck2x3" id="karma2018205ckNxM"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column" id="dd2018205" sticky-container=""><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;" v-sticky=""><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1897248">forumgames</b><span class="vote-button-legend" content="2024-01-02" itemprop="datePublished" style="padding: 0 1rem;">01/02/24 16:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div itemprop="reviewBody" v-pre=""><p>Beautiful perfume, very gourmand and sweet.<br/>
I expected this to be way more lactonic, instead I feel like it leans more towards sugary sweet.<br/>
<br/>
Impressive sillage and lasting power, lasts all day and projects for at least 6-8 hours.<br/>
I become nose blind to the scent trail, I can't smell it while moving etc, but people are always complimenting me or asking what I'm wearing even if they don't get too close to me.<br/>
I pick this perfume if I know that I won't be able to reapply during the day. <br/>
<br/>
It reminds me a little bit of Pink Sugar but more grown up, definitely higher quality and a little more complex.<br/>
A cashier asked me if I was wearing pink sugar because her teenage daughter bathes herself in it and she could recognize some similarities whitin the scent. I agree that they might be similar but they're not the same thing at all. <br/>
<br/>
This fragrance is VERY sweet, I like it but for some it might be offensive or too sweet and cloying. It might also be slighty synthetic but it doesn't bother me at all.<br/>
<br/>
I'm addicted to Bianco Latte, from opening to drydown.<br/>
The caramel is absolutely yummy and I need to fight the urge to eat my arm.<br/>
The honey is mothwatering and the drydown is the sweetest and tastier vanilla ever.<br/>
There's also something "clean" about this fragrance, it's sweet and gourmand but gives a very clean creamy vibe, this is something that I pick up myself but it has been said from others as well, I think that Musk is responsible for this. I'm a white musk lover so this is definitely a plus for me. <br/>
<br/>
I love this fragrance, for now this is my favourite perfume and I find it absolutely addictive.<br/>

The hype is real. It is vanilla goodness sprinkled with a hefty dose of coumarin. It comes across as vanilla-bitter almond for me, so good! I have so many fragrances in my collection but I can't seem to put it down, there is literally no day when I don't come to my perfume shelf and give it a sniff or spray. As for the reformulation I don't think it is a case. I've been testing Bianco Latte from 3 different bottles with different batches and I don't seem to notice that it is weaker or anything. As the time progresses and it macerates it is a beast mode. This perfume is simple but it has some magic in it. Maybe mine was a bad decant but it is very alcohol heavy at first spray so I suggest letting it sit for a while to dry down into the gourmand goodness it really is! Perfume was also really plasticky at first but after letting it macerate and sit for a day it was fine! Definitely hold onto the dry down in my opinion, after that its sweet delicious sailing :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="2003531" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=2003531#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent2003470" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":0,"winter":0,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":0,"sillage":0,"gender":null,"relation":null}'></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Unfortunately I blind bought this because I love Gourmands and laconic scents, but this is a hard pass.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="1998926" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=1998926#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent1998827" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":4,"winter":1,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":1,"day":1,"night":0,"longevity":5,"sillage":2,"gender":"female","relation":"have"}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="4" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Super gourmand, the most gourmand.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="1992622" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=1992622#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent1992571" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":0,"winter":0,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":0,"day":0,"night":0,"longevity":0,"sillage":0,"gender":null,"relation":null}'></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br/>

<br/>

<br/>
EDIT: After using this for about a week I've changed my mind about it being replaceable by Vanille Coco. The first spray of both is quite similar, but the dry downs are very different. Vanille Coco stays pretty linear and has more summer vibes, but Bianco Latte is thicker and has more complexity and layers. To think something is so thick and waxy while being sexy and grown?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="1888594" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=1888594#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent1697879" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":5,"winter":1,"spring":0,"summer":0,"autumn":1,"day":1,"night":1,"longevity":4,"sillage":1,"gender":"female","relation":"have"}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="5" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is overwhelmingly synthetic immediately upon spraying, an alcoholic assault of milky liquer, but that quickly dissipates in seconds. Upon warming on the skin, the fragrance opens up, creating an intimate scent bubble and you are enveloped in that milky, musky vanilla cloud described by the brand. Vanilla is the main player here, with some whispers of caramel and suggestions of warmed milk. Vanilla and musk stay detectable on the skin for 6+ hours. It lasts eternally on clothing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="1697879" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=1697879#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" id="parent1810190" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);"><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes='{"rating":5,"winter":0,"spring":1,"summer":0,"autumn":1,"day":1,"night":0,"longevity":0,"sillage":0,"gender":"unisex","relation":"want"}'><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating"><meta content="5" itemprop="ratingValue"/><meta content="5" itemprop="bestRating"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div class="cell small-2" id="cc1810190" sticky-container=""><div v-sticky=""><div class="comments-avatar" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" style="position: relative;"><meta content="HER30" itemprop="name"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1392691"><img alt="HER30" class="comments-avatar" itemprop="image" loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" style="opacity: 0.85;"/></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div class="ckNxM ck4x2" id="karma1810190ckNxM"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column" id="dd1810190" sticky-container=""><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;" v-sticky=""><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1392691">HER30</b><span class="vote-button-legend" content="2023-04-16" itemprop="datePublished" style="padding: 0 1rem;">04/16/23 08:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div itemprop="reviewBody" v-pre=""><p>Just what I was looking for! Next to my other vanillas this is "light," but allow me to explain: It's not light on performance/projection - it stays consistent and projects well. It's light in the sense that it is not a deep dark heavy vanilla with lots of spice or patchouli. Some other vanillas conjure more of a vanilla extract or dark vanilla bean vibe. This smells like "whiter lighter" vanilla. Think steaming milk with caramel, or milk and honey, or a white cakey vanilla. It's of course sweet - but it's not overly sweet to my nose. It is approachable and yummy but with enough depth and interest that it is not a simple linear vanilla (like Fire at Will). It is totally made for a woman or man, not childish in any way. I would not even layer this one because of its lovely complexity on its own. It's a versatile gourmand fine for different seasons or situations, but would love this delicious cozy fragrance in the Fall. Since I just discovered it though, I'll be wearing it all this Spring! So lovely and I think more than "meets the eye" with this one if you compare it to some other vanillas and sit with it for a bit. It's not loud, just stunning.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons comment_id="1810190" initial_status="neutral" item_id="64757" vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html?ccid=1810190#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div> <reviews-infinity :perfume-id="64757" :random-colors='["#fefcee","#faf7ec","#f9f9f3","#f8f9ec","#fffdea","#faf9fb","#faf5f2","#f7f4f2"]' sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
